name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr

posted:Posted July 17, 2023
msg:There are 2 hotels in the scenic area of ‚Äã‚ÄãYudao, one is a resort hotel and the other is a hot spring hotel. The hot spring private hot spring room needs to be checked in at the resort hotel. The room is inside the exit of the hot spring hotel towards the beach, where you can have breakfast and soak indoors Hot springs are very convenient. The room is very close to the sea, at most 2 minutes walk. It is far away from the free expansion facilities in the scenic area, Hobbit Paradise and other areas. Advantages: The room has complete facilities, 4 bottles of mineral water per day, the house is big enough, 2 big and 2 small can be very comfortable, and it is very close to hot springs and the sea. The private soup in the room is downstairs, which is very large, and there is no pressure to soak 2 big and 2 small. Scenic spots: Check in the hotel to send tickets to the scenic spot. There is a playground in the Yudao scenic spot. Most of the facilities require more than 140cm, and half of them are 120+, such as pirate ships. Few can play below 100cm. There is a Ferris wheel, and the facilities may be closed due to weather. . There are various performances in the scenic area, please refer to the performance time in the photo. There is an outdoor water park with various slides. Grass skiing. There is a small train in the scenic area, and you can ride it for free with your room card or scenic spot tickets. In fact, the distance between each area is not far, and you can walk within 10 minutes. Scenic shuttle bus charges 35 yuan per trip. Catering: The hotel's breakfast buffet is definitely different from the high-star hotels in Aranya, but it is still clean and full. Most of the scenic spots are snacks and light meals. If you need to eat seafood, it is recommended to drive there. The hotel is 5-10 minutes by car from the exit of the scenic spot. Without a car, it is very troublesome to go out to eat. There are various restaurants for western food and light meals by the sea. Hot spring: During the stay, the hot spring can be entered and exited many times. When you check out, you will return your hand card, and you will not be able to enter the hot spring again. If you check out at 9 o'clock the next day, you can choose to give away tickets to scenic spots or hot springs, and you will get nothing if you check out at 12 o'clock. There are many indoor hot spring pools with various temperatures, and there is also a special wave pool for which you need to wear a swimming cap. If the weather is bad and the beach baths are closed, the number of hot springs will increase dramatically. Slippery, slippery, slippery. There is a slide pool specially for children under 140cm, and there are staff to remind and supervise at any time, and the overall order is very good. There is also a relatively large swimming pool outdoors, with plenty of sunlight and good water quality. Seaside: Super close. The beach will be open according to the weather. When swimming is not open, you can also dig sand and wade in the water. The beach has a powder sand beach specially used for taking pictures, which requires a separate ticket. The beach has tents (150 yuan a day), cloth umbrellas (200 yuan a day), and wooden umbrellas (150 yuan for 2 hours) that can be rented. There will be rubbish, but overall it is fairly clean. The management personnel are very responsible and always remind of high tide or other dangers. The overall physical examination is very good. With the Aranya club already costing 3000+ per night, this place is very cost-effective.

The various play points are not too far away. Of course, when the weather is hot and I am tired from playing, it will take a while to walk. That little train is actually me. I don‚Äôt recommend it very much, but the 20-bit/time small battery I feel tired can sit for a while, especially from the entrance of the scenic spot to the pink beach or the return journey from the pink beach to the gate, it is convenient to have it at any time. About 100 meters away from the gate of the scenic spot on the right hand is the Valley of Flowers. It is good to take pictures and punch cards. Opposite is the venue of Hollywood stunt performances. The Hollywood stunt performances are very beautiful, the scenes and plots are in place, and the performances of foreign actors are also wonderful and worth watching. Going down about 100 meters is the Witches Playground and Water Park next to each other. 50 meters next to the water park is the hot spring resort hotel. The first floor is for reception and check-in, the second floor is for restaurants and indoor hot springs, and the third floor and 3E are guest rooms. Various paddling areas and surfing pools. In addition, there is a door at the back of the indoor hot spring to go to the outdoor area behind the hot spring hotel. There are also outdoor hot spring pools and swimming pools, and there is also a spiral hovercraft slide with a weight limit of 90 to 180 pounds. . Go out the front door of the hot spring resort and walk around the hotel for a few dozen meters, or the back door of the outdoor hot spring is the pink beach. The sand is very fine, the sea water is very clean, and it is shallow, the water is not deep, there are special security guards on the shore, the beach There are several areas separated by seat belts, and it is also safe for children to play in the water. The hot spring pool by the sea is the punch-in place for Internet celebrities to take pictures. But the most convenient point of staying in the hotel is that you can go back to rest when you are tired from playing. You can go to the beach to take pictures after 8:00 in the morning. The tourists have not yet entered the park, so it is very quiet and comfortable. I feel that the whole scenic spot is for myself. Speaking of check-in, it must be said that if the scenic spot has booked a room on the day, the requirement is to check in after 14:00, but if you arrive early, there is a reception desk dedicated to check-in on the south side of the gate of the scenic spot (you can ask the security guard in command), which will give you You have a special ticket, and then you can drive into the scenic spot from gate 2, and then you can play in the scenic spot in advance with this paper ticket, and then wait until 14:00 to check in. After check-in, you can show the room card (room Limit a few people to a few room cards) to play all kinds of amu*****t facilities indefinitely. Last but not least, the breakfast is very rich and delicious. Overall, I am very satisfied with the day's play and stay experience, and I will come again in the future!
